# Trak - Complete Booking Automation System
## Specification Document v2.0
### Date: January 13, 2026

---

# 1. VISION

Trak transforms from a CRM into a **full-funnel automation platform for Serbian travel agencies**.

**The Problem:**
Travel agencies in Serbia manually handle inquiries via Viber, phone, and email. They lose leads, forget follow-ups, and have no system for converting interest into bookings.

**The Solution:**
One platform that handles: Ad â†’ Qualification â†’ Offer Matching â†’ Reservation â†’ Payment â†’ Contract â†’ Follow-up

**Positioning:**
"Shopify for Travel Agencies" - They don't need a website, booking system, payment processor, or CRM. They just need Trak.

---

## 2.2 Two Inventory Types â­ NEW IN v2.0

Serbian travel agencies have **two distinct types of offers**:

| Type | Code | Serbian | Description | Customer Flow |
|------|------|---------|-------------|---------------|
| **Owned/Contracted** | `owned` | Sopstveni kapacitet | Apartments/rooms agency pre-bought for the season | Instant reservation with 72h hold |
| **On-Request** | `inquiry` | Na upit | Offers they list but must verify with supplier | Inquiry â†’ Agent checks â†’ Response |

### Key Differences

| Aspect | Owned (Instant) | Inquiry (On-Request) |
|--------|-----------------|----------------------|
| Capacity display | âœ… Show bar + X/Y | âŒ Hidden |
| Capacity accuracy | 100% accurate | N/A |
| Price accuracy | 100% | 99% (rarely changes) |
| CTA button | "RezerviÅ¡i odmah" | "PoÅ¡alji upit" |
| After click | Reservation form (72h hold) | Simple inquiry form |
| Response time | Instant | Dynamic (10min / next working day) |

### Database Field
```sql
ALTER TABLE offers ADD COLUMN inventory_type VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'inquiry';
-- Values: 'owned' or 'inquiry'
```

### Updated Results Page Flow

After qualification, results are split into **two sections**:

### Dynamic Response Time Display

Response time message changes based on **agency working hours**:

| Scenario | Message | Icon |
|----------|---------|------|
| During working hours | "Odgovor u roku od 10 minuta" | âš¡ |
| After hours, opens tomorrow | "Odgovaramo sutra od 09:00" | ğŸŒ™ |
| After hours, opens Monday | "Odgovaramo u ponedeljak od 09:00" | ğŸ“… |
| Early morning before open | "Odgovaramo od 09:00" | â˜€ï¸ |

Working hours are configurable per agency (see Section 13.1 - Agency Settings).

### Inquiry Rules

- **Single inquiry only** - Customer can only send one inquiry at a time
- **Show alternatives** - After submitting inquiry, show instant-booking offers
- **Agent notification** - Agent gets notified immediately of new inquiries
- **Conversion flow** - If available, agent creates reservation â†’ customer gets email
- **Unavailable flow** - Agent marks unavailable â†’ customer gets alternative suggestions

---

## 3.6 Qualification Summary

**Time Breakdown:**
| Step | Action | Time |
|------|--------|------|
| 1 | Tap country | 2s |
| 2 | Tap city or "Svejedno" | 2s |
| 3 | Tap adults | 1s |
| 4 | Tap kids + ages | 3s |
| 5 | Tap month | 1s |
| 6 | Tap duration | 1s |
| 7 | Tap accommodation type | 2s |
| 8 | Tap board | 2s |
| 9 | Tap transport | 1s |
| 10 | Tap budget | 2s |
| **TOTAL** | | **~17 seconds** |

**Data Collected:**
```typescript
interface QualificationData {
  destination: {
    country: string;
    city: string | null;
  };
  guests: {
    adults: number;
    children: number;
    childAges: number[];
  };
  dates: {
    month: string | null;
    exactStart: Date | null;
    exactEnd: Date | null;
    duration: number; // nights
    flexible: boolean;
  };
  accommodation: {
    type: 'hotel' | 'apartment' | 'villa' | 'any';
    board: 'all_inclusive' | 'half_board' | 'breakfast' | 'room_only' | 'any';
    transport: 'included' | 'own';
  };
  budget: {
    min: number | null;
    max: number | null;
    perPerson: boolean;
  };
}
```

---

# 4. DATA ENTRY & LEAD CAPTURE

## 4.1 Entry Channels Overview

| Channel | Entry Method | Time | Effort |
|---------|--------------|------|--------|
| Facebook/IG Ads | Webhook â†’ auto-create | 0 sec | None |
| Trak Form/Chat | Already in system | 0 sec | None |
| FB/IG DMs | Click â†’ AI extract â†’ Save | 5 sec | 1 click |
| Email (forwarded) | Auto (AI parse) | 2 sec | Forward email |
| Viber/WhatsApp | Paste message â†’ AI extract | 5 sec | Copy-paste |
| Phone call | Quick tap form | 15 sec | Manual |
| Voice memo | Record â†’ AI extract | 10 sec | Record + click |

## 4.5 Email Forwarding

Agency gets assigned address: `agencija@trak.rs`

They forward any inquiry email there â†’ AI parses â†’ Creates lead â†’ Agent notified.

## 4.6 Phone Number = Identity

Once phone number entered, Trak can:

1. **Auto-link repeat customers** - "Marko se vratio! ProÅ¡le godine bio u GrÄkoj."
2. **Show conversation history** - All past inquiries from this number
3. **Click to call/WhatsApp/Viber** - One tap to contact
4. **Duplicate detection** - "Ovaj broj veÄ‡ postoji u sistemu"

---

# 5. BOOKING & CLOSING FLOW

## 5.1 Why This Matters

If bookings via Viber/phone aren't entered, capacity is wrong:

```
Offer: Hotel Azul, 12 spots

Reality:
- 3 booked via Trak âœ“ (system knows)
- 5 booked via Viber/phone âœ— (system doesn't know)

System shows: "10 mesta" âŒ
Actual: "4 mesta" âœ…
```

**Every booking MUST go through Trak for capacity to be accurate.**

**What happens on cancellation:**

1. âœ… Booking status â†’ "cancelled"
2. âœ… Spots return to offer (automatic)
3. âœ… Cancellation reason logged
4. âœ… Refund amount tracked
5. âœ… Lead status â†’ "Otkazano" (new stage) or back to pipeline

## 5.8 Overbooking Prevention

System does NOT allow booking past 0 available spots:

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

## 5.9 Entry Time Summary

| Scenario | Entry Time |
|----------|------------|
| Lead from Trak â†’ closes via system | Auto (already linked) |
| Lead exists â†’ quick close | 5 sec (select offer, confirm) |
| Pipeline drag â†’ close | 5 sec |
| Direct booking (no lead) | 15 sec |
| External booking | 20 sec |


### Results Page: Label Distribution Example

For 8 offers shown, aim for approximately:
- 1-2 with red urgency (ğŸ”¥ Poslednja mesta / â° IstiÄe)
- 1-2 with orange/green signals (ğŸ“ˆ Popunjava se / ğŸ’° SniÅ¾eno)
- 0-1 with soft signals (ğŸ†• Novo / â­ Popularno / ğŸ‘ PreporuÄujemo)
- 3-4 with no label (normal offers)

**Result: ~50% with labels, ~50% without**

## 6.2 Urgency & Value Labels System

### Design Principle
**Always show urgency/value labels on ~50% of offers.** This creates contrast - if everything is urgent, nothing is. Labels should help users decide, not overwhelm them.

### Label Hierarchy (Priority Order)

Labels are assigned automatically based on data. Only ONE label per offer, highest priority wins:

| Priority | Label | Trigger Condition | Color | Icon |
|----------|-------|------------------|-------|------|
| 1 | **POSLEDNJA MESTA** | available_spots â‰¤ 2 | Red #EF4444 | ğŸ”¥ |
| 2 | **ISTIÄŒE USKORO** | departure_date - today â‰¤ 7 days | Red #EF4444 | â° |
| 3 | **POPUNJAVA SE** | booked â‰¥ 70% AND available > 2 | Orange #F97316 | ğŸ“ˆ |
| 4 | **SNIÅ½ENO -X%** | original_price > price (show %) | Green #10B981 | ğŸ’° |
| 5 | **NOVO** | created_at within 7 days | Purple #8B5CF6 | ğŸ†• |
| 6 | **POPULARNO** | â‰¥10 views in last 24h | Blue #3B82F6 | â­ |
| 7 | **PREPORUÄŒUJEMO** | is_recommended = true (manual) | Blue #3B82F6 | ğŸ‘ |
| - | *No label* | None of above | - | - |

### Automatic Label Assignment Logic

```typescript
function getOfferLabel(offer: Offer): Label | null {
  const today = new Date();
  const daysUntilDeparture = daysBetween(today, offer.departure_date);
  const bookedPercentage = ((offer.total_spots - offer.available_spots) / offer.total_spots) * 100;
  const daysSinceCreated = daysBetween(offer.created_at, today);
  const hasDiscount = offer.original_price && offer.original_price > offer.price_per_person;
  const discountPercent = hasDiscount 
    ? Math.round((1 - offer.price_per_person / offer.original_price) * 100) 
    : 0;

  // Priority 1: Last spots (ONLY when â‰¤2)
  if (offer.available_spots <= 2 && offer.available_spots > 0) {
    return { 
      type: 'POSLEDNJA_MESTA', 
      text: `JoÅ¡ samo ${offer.available_spots}!`,
      color: 'red',
      icon: 'ğŸ”¥'
    };
  }

  // Priority 2: Departing very soon
  if (daysUntilDeparture <= 7 && daysUntilDeparture > 0) {
    return { 
      type: 'ISTICE_USKORO', 
      text: daysUntilDeparture <= 3 ? 'Polazak za par dana!' : 'Uskoro polazak',
      color: 'red',
      icon: 'â°'
    };
  }

  // Priority 3: Filling up fast
  if (bookedPercentage >= 70 && offer.available_spots > 2) {
    return { 
      type: 'POPUNJAVA_SE', 
      text: 'Popunjava se brzo',
      color: 'orange',
      icon: 'ğŸ“ˆ'
    };
  }

  // Priority 4: Has discount
  if (hasDiscount && discountPercent >= 10) {
    return { 
      type: 'SNIZENO', 
      text: `-${discountPercent}%`,
      color: 'green',
      icon: 'ğŸ’°'
    };
  }

  // Priority 5: New offer
  if (daysSinceCreated <= 7) {
    return { 
      type: 'NOVO', 
      text: 'Novo',
      color: 'purple',
      icon: 'ğŸ†•'
    };
  }

  // Priority 6: Popular (high engagement)
  if (offer.views_last_24h >= 10) {
    return { 
      type: 'POPULARNO', 
      text: 'Popularno',
      color: 'blue',
      icon: 'â­'
    };
  }

  // Priority 7: Manual recommendation
  if (offer.is_recommended) {
    return { 
      type: 'PREPORUCUJEMO', 
      text: 'PreporuÄujemo',
      color: 'blue',
      icon: 'ğŸ‘'
    };
  }

  // No label
  return null;
}
```

### Ensuring 50% Label Coverage

If automatic labels cover <50% of displayed offers, the system should:

1. **Auto-promote to "PreporuÄujemo"** - Offers with highest booking rate or best value (price vs. star rating)
2. **Show subtle value indicators** - Even without a badge, show things like "OdliÄna vrednost" in smaller text

```typescript
function ensureLabelCoverage(offers: Offer[]): Offer[] {
  const withLabels = offers.filter(o => getOfferLabel(o) !== null);
  const withoutLabels = offers.filter(o => getOfferLabel(o) === null);
  
  const targetWithLabels = Math.ceil(offers.length * 0.5);
  const needMore = targetWithLabels - withLabels.length;
  
  if (needMore > 0) {
    // Sort unlabeled by value score (price per star, booking rate, etc.)
    const sorted = withoutLabels.sort((a, b) => getValueScore(b) - getValueScore(a));
    
    // Mark top ones as recommended
    sorted.slice(0, needMore).forEach(offer => {
      offer.is_recommended = true; // Temporary flag for display
    });
  }
  
  return offers;
}
```

### Label Display Rules

| Scenario | What to Show |
|----------|--------------|
| available_spots = 0 | "RASPRODATO" (grayed out, not clickable) |
| available_spots = 1 | "ğŸ”¥ POSLEDNJE MESTO!" |
| available_spots = 2 | "ğŸ”¥ JOÅ  SAMO 2!" |
| available_spots = 3-5 AND >70% booked | "ğŸ“ˆ POPUNJAVA SE" |
| available_spots > 5 AND >70% booked | "ğŸ“ˆ POPUNJAVA SE" |
| discount â‰¥ 20% | "ğŸ’° -25% SNIÅ½ENO" (highlight strongly) |
| discount 10-19% | "ğŸ’° -15%" (subtle) |
| discount < 10% | Don't show discount label |


### What NOT to Do

âŒ Don't show "POSLEDNJA MESTA" if >2 spots remain (loses trust)
âŒ Don't show multiple labels on one offer (confusing)
âŒ Don't show urgency on >60% of offers (numbs the effect)
âŒ Don't fake urgency (e.g., fake countdown timers)
âŒ Don't show "NOVO" on offers older than 7 days

## 6.3 Capacity Bar

**Only show capacity bar when it adds urgency** (â‰¥50% booked). Don't show for mostly empty offers.

```
< 50% booked:    [Don't show bar - no urgency signal]

50-69% booked:   â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘ 5/10 mesta          Gray #94A3B8
                 "JoÅ¡ ima mesta"

70-89% booked:   â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘ 7/10 mesta          Orange #F97316
                 "Popunjava se"

90-99% booked:   â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘ 9/10 mesta          Red #EF4444
                 "Skoro popunjeno"

Last 2:          â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆ JoÅ¡ samo 2!         Red #EF4444 (pulsing)

Last 1:          â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆ POSLEDNJE MESTO!    Red #EF4444 (pulsing)

Sold out:        â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆ Rasprodato          Gray #94A3B8 (disabled)
```

### Capacity Bar Logic

```typescript
function shouldShowCapacityBar(offer: Offer): boolean {
  const bookedPercent = ((offer.total_spots - offer.available_spots) / offer.total_spots) * 100;
  return bookedPercent >= 50 || offer.available_spots <= 3;
}

function getCapacityBarStyle(offer: Offer) {
  const available = offer.available_spots;
  const bookedPercent = ((offer.total_spots - available) / offer.total_spots) * 100;

  if (available === 0) return { color: 'gray', text: 'Rasprodato', pulse: false };
  if (available === 1) return { color: 'red', text: 'POSLEDNJE MESTO!', pulse: true };
  if (available === 2) return { color: 'red', text: 'JoÅ¡ samo 2!', pulse: true };
  if (bookedPercent >= 90) return { color: 'red', text: 'Skoro popunjeno', pulse: false };
  if (bookedPercent >= 70) return { color: 'orange', text: 'Popunjava se', pulse: false };
  if (bookedPercent >= 50) return { color: 'gray', text: 'JoÅ¡ ima mesta', pulse: false };
  
  return null; // Don't show bar
}
```

## 7.2 Payment Options

| Option | Description | What Happens |
|--------|-------------|--------------|
| **Avans 20%** | Pay deposit now via card | Price locked, contract sent immediately |
| **Pun iznos** | Pay full amount now | Contract sent, booking confirmed |
| **U agenciji** | Reserve now, pay later at office | Agent contacts to arrange visit |
| **Kontakt** | Just want to talk | Agent calls within 1 hour |

## 7.3 Reservation Hold Time

**Standard: 72 hours**

```
Reservation made â†’ 72h countdown starts
                 â†“
              +24h: Email reminder "IstiÄe za 48h"
                 â†“
              +48h: Email reminder "Poslednji dan!"
                 â†“
              +72h: Reservation expires
                   OR
                   Payment received â†’ Confirmed âœ“
```

### Notification Types

| Event | Icon | When | Agent Action |
|-------|------|------|--------------|
| New lead | ğŸ†• | Lead created (any channel) | View, Contact |
| New reservation | âœ… | Customer reserves offer | View, Call |
| Payment received | ğŸ’³ | Any payment comes in | Send contract |
| Reservation expiring | â° | 24h, 12h, 1h before expiry | Call, Extend |
| Reservation expired | âŒ | 72h passed, no payment | Return to pipeline |
| Booking cancelled | ğŸš« | Customer cancels | View details |
| New message | ğŸ’¬ | FB/IG/Messenger message | Reply, Create lead |

### Delivery Channels

- **In-app** - Always (bell icon, counter badge)
- **Email** - Configurable per event type
- **Browser push** - If enabled
- **Mobile push** - When mobile app exists

| Event | Icon | When | Agent Action |
|-------|------|------|--------------|
| New inquiry | ğŸ“‹ | Customer submits inquiry | Check availability |
| Inquiry waiting | â° | No response in 10+ min | Urgent: respond |
| Inquiry converted | âœ… | Marked as available | Reservation created |
| Inquiry closed | âŒ | Marked as unavailable | Alternative sent |

## 9.4 Daily Reconciliation System

Ensures agents don't leave without recording all bookings. If bookings made via phone/Viber aren't entered, capacity tracking breaks.

### 9.3.5 Reconciliation Schedule

| When | What | Who | Required? |
|------|------|-----|-----------|
| 17:00 daily | Soft reminder popup | Agent | No (dismissable) |
| 9:00 next day | "Anything from yesterday?" | Agent | **Yes (blocker)** |
| Weekly (Sunday) | Capacity audit for hot offers | Manager | Configurable |

### 9.3.6 Tracking Reconciliation Compliance

System tracks if agents are adding bookings after confirming "sve je uneseno":

```

â€¢ 5 dana potvrdila da je sve uneseno
â€¢ 2 puta dodala prodaju POSLE potvrde âš ï¸

â†’ MoÅ¾da treba podseÄ‡anje da bolje proverava
```

# 10. ARANÅ½MANI (Trip Management)

## 10.1 Concept: Trip-Centric vs Person-Centric

Traditional CRM tracks **people** through stages. Trak groups **people by trip** - because that's how agencies actually work.

**Why trip-centric:**

| Person-Centric | Trip-Centric |
|----------------|--------------|
| "Milan needs payment" | "Hanioti trip has 3 people with issues" |
| Can't see group size | See 8/12 booked at a glance |
| Prepare docs one by one | Prepare all vouchers for trip at once |
| No trip overview | See trip health instantly |
| Emergency? Search everyone | Emergency? Click trip â†’ see all contacts |

**Trip is created automatically** when the first traveler books a specific offer for a specific date.

## 10.2 Layout: Kanban/Vertical

Trips are **columns** (horizontal scroll), travelers are **cards** stacked vertically within each column.

Consistent with Pipeline view for leads.

**Sorting:** Nearest departure first (ascending by departure_date).


| Tab | Shows | When to use |
|-----|-------|-------------|
| **Svi** | All active trips | DEFAULT - overview with color coding |
| **Priprema** | Trips with at least one issue | Focus on problems only |
| **Spremno** | Trips where everything is OK | Pre-departure verification |
| **Na putu** | Currently traveling | Emergencies |
| **VraÄ‡eni** | Completed, awaiting archive | Post-trip follow-up |

### Collapse/Expand Logic

| Traveler count | Display |
|----------------|---------|
| 1-4 | All cards visible, no collapse |
| 5+ | Show first 3 cards + expand button |

### Checklist Icons

| Icon | Color | Meaning |
|------|-------|---------|
| âœ“ | Green background | Completed |
| âš  or ! | Orange background | Issue - action needed |
| â—‹ | Gray background | Not yet (but not urgent) |

**Note:** No avatars. Name and phone are sufficient for identification.

## 10.6 Trip-Level Actions

Bulk actions for the entire trip:

| Action | Description | When to use |
|--------|-------------|-------------|
| Svi voucheri | Generate vouchers for all travelers at once | Before departure |
| PoÅ¡alji info svima | Send departure info email to all travelers | 3-7 days before departure |
| Lista putnika | Export manifest (PDF/Excel) for hotel/transport | Before departure |
| Kontakti | List of all phone numbers for this trip | During travel |
| Info o hotelu | Quick access to hotel contact | During travel |

**Actions shown depend on status:**

| Status | Actions shown |
|--------|---------------|
| Priprema | Voucheri, PoÅ¡alji info, Lista |
| Spremno | Voucheri, PoÅ¡alji info, Lista |
| Na putu | Kontakti, Info o hotelu |
| VraÄ‡eni | (archive only) |

## 10.7 Views

| View | Shows | Best for |
|------|-------|----------|
| **Kanban (default)** | Columns = trips, cards = travelers | Daily management |
| **Problemi** | Only trips/travelers with issues | Morning check |
| **Kalendar** | Timeline of departures | Planning ahead |

## 10.8 Color System

### Principle: Color is Earned

Default is neutral. Color is only used when it carries information.

### Trip Column - Top Border (4px)

| Color | Hex | Meaning |
|-------|-----|---------|
| Blue | #3b82f6 | Default - trip in preparation, all OK |
| Orange | #f59e0b | Trip has at least one issue |
| Green | #22c55e | Trip currently traveling |

### Traveler Card - Left Border (3px)

| Color | Hex | Meaning |
|-------|-----|---------|
| Green | #22c55e | All OK - paid, documents, voucher |
| Orange | #f59e0b | Has issue - awaiting payment/document |
| Gray | #e2e8f0 | Default / neutral |

### Status Badge

| Text | Background | Text Color | When |
|------|------------|------------|------|
| âœ“ PlaÄ‡eno | #dcfce7 (light green) | #166534 (dark green) | Fully paid |
| âœ“ Na putu | #dcfce7 | #166534 | Currently traveling |
| ÄŒeka uplatu | #fef3c7 (light orange) | #92400e (dark orange) | Has remainder |
| ÄŒeka pasoÅ¡ | #fef3c7 | #92400e | Missing document |
| ÄŒeka dokument | #fef3c7 | #92400e | Missing document |

### Issues Banner (in trip column)

| Text | Background | Text Color |
|------|------------|------------|
| âœ“ Sve spremno | #dcfce7 | #166534 |
| âš  X Äeka uplatu... | #fef3c7 | #92400e |

### Checklist Icons

| Icon | Background | Icon Color | Meaning |
|------|------------|------------|---------|
| âœ“ | #dcfce7 | #16a34a | Completed |
| ! or âš  | #fef3c7 | #d97706 | Issue |
| â—‹ | #f1f5f9 | #94a3b8 | Not yet |

### What Has NO Color (stays neutral/gray)

- Avatars (we don't use them)
- Icons in stats bar (only background has color)
- Footer action buttons
- Text except status badges
- Countdown (unless < 7 days WITH issue)

| Status | Conditions | Actions |
|--------|------------|---------|
| **Priprema** | Has at least one incomplete checklist item | Payment, documents, vouchers, info |
| **Spremno** | All checklist items complete, before departure date | Verification, last-minute changes |
| **Na putu** | Departure date passed, return date not yet | Emergency contact, hotel info |
| **VraÄ‡eni** | Return date passed | Follow-up, satisfaction survey |
| **Arhivirano** | Manually archived or auto after X days | History |

# 13. AI FEATURES â­ NEW IN v2.0

## 13.1 Overview

TRAK uses AI to automate tedious tasks and improve conversion rates. All AI features use Claude (Anthropic) or GPT-4o (OpenAI) APIs.

| # | Feature | Phase | Always On | Cost/Agency |
|---|---------|-------|-----------|-------------|
| 1 | Message Parsing | 2 | âœ… | ~â‚¬2/month |
| 2 | Screenshot OCR | 2 | âœ… | ~â‚¬1/month |
| 3 | Smart Offer Matching | 3 | âœ… | ~â‚¬3/month |
| 4 | Lead Scoring | 3 | âœ… | ~â‚¬1/month |
| 5 | Abandoned Cart Emails | 3 | âš™ï¸ Opt-in | ~â‚¬2/month |

**Total: ~â‚¬9/month per agency** (<2.5% of subscription)

---

## 13.2 Message Parsing ("Brzi unos")

Agent pastes Viber/WhatsApp message, AI extracts structured data.

### Input/Output

```
INPUT (pasted text):
"Zdravo, zanima me GrÄka za 4 osobe negde u julu, 
budÅ¾et oko 500e po osobi. Javite mi se na 064 123 4567. Marko"

OUTPUT (structured):
{
  "name": "Marko",
  "phone": "064 123 4567",
  "destination": "GrÄka",
  "guests": 4,
  "date": "Jul",
  "budget": "â‚¬500/os",
  "confidence": 0.95
}
```

### Implementation

```typescript
async function parseMessage(message: string): Promise<LeadData> {
  // 1. Try regex first (instant, free)
  const basic = extractWithRegex(message);
  
  // 2. If phone + destination found, good enough
  if (basic.phone && basic.destination) {
    return basic;
  }
  
  // 3. Use AI for complex messages
  const response = await anthropic.messages.create({
    model: "claude-3-haiku-20240307",
    max_tokens: 256,
    messages: [{
      role: "user",
      content: `Extract travel inquiry data from this Serbian message.
        Return JSON only: {name, phone, destination, guests, date, budget}
        
        Message: "${message}"`
    }]
  });
  
  return JSON.parse(response.content[0].text);
}
```

### Fallback Strategy

```
Message received
    â”‚
    â”œâ”€â†’ Regex extraction (instant, free)
    â”‚   â”œâ”€â†’ Found phone + destination? â†’ Use regex result
    â”‚   â””â”€â†’ Missing key fields? â†’ Continue to AI
    â”‚
    â”œâ”€â†’ AI extraction (Claude Haiku)
    â”‚   â”œâ”€â†’ Success? â†’ Use AI result
    â”‚   â””â”€â†’ Failed/timeout? â†’ Return partial + flag for review
    â”‚
    â””â”€â†’ Agent manually completes missing fields
```

---


### Implementation

```typescript
async function parseScreenshot(imageBase64: string): Promise<LeadData> {
  const response = await anthropic.messages.create({
    model: "claude-3-haiku-20240307",
    max_tokens: 512,
    messages: [{
      role: "user",
      content: [
        {
          type: "image",
          source: { type: "base64", media_type: "image/png", data: imageBase64 }
        },
        {
          type: "text",
          text: `This is a screenshot of a Serbian travel inquiry chat.
            Extract: {name, phone, destination, guests, date, budget}
            Return JSON only.`
        }
      ]
    }]
  });
  
  return JSON.parse(response.content[0].text);
}
```

## 13.4 Smart Offer Matching

Beyond simple filters, AI ranks offers based on multiple signals.

### Ranking Signals

| Signal | Weight | Description |
|--------|--------|-------------|
| Filter match | 40% | Matches qualification criteria |
| Margin | 20% | Higher margin offers ranked up |
| Inventory urgency | 15% | Low stock = higher rank |
| Popularity | 10% | High views/bookings |
| Seasonal fit | 10% | Peak season popularity |
| Similar bookings | 5% | What similar customers booked |

### Output

```typescript
interface RankedOffer {
  offer_id: string;
  match_score: number;      // 0-100
  rank_reasons: string[];   // ["TaÄna destinacija", "U okviru budÅ¾eta", "Popularan"]
}

// Example output
[
  { offer_id: "abc", match_score: 95, rank_reasons: ["TaÄna destinacija", "All Inclusive", "Visoka popularnost"] },
  { offer_id: "def", match_score: 87, rank_reasons: ["SliÄna destinacija", "U budÅ¾etu", "Poslednja 3 mesta"] },
  { offer_id: "ghi", match_score: 82, rank_reasons: ["PreporuÄeno", "OdliÄna vrednost"] }
]
```

---

## 13.5 Lead Scoring

AI predicts conversion probability based on lead attributes.

### Input Signals

| Signal | Impact |
|--------|--------|
| Source (Facebook Ad vs Organic) | High |
| Budget clarity ("â‚¬500" vs "nije bitno") | High |
| Response time (how fast they replied) | Medium |
| Specificity (exact dates vs "negde u julu") | Medium |
| Guest count (2 vs 6+) | Low |
| Repeat customer | High |

### Output

```typescript
interface LeadScore {
  score: number;           // 0-100
  conversion_probability: number;  // 0.0-1.0
  signals: {
    positive: string[];    // ["Jasan budÅ¾et", "TaÄan datum", "Povratni kupac"]
    negative: string[];    // ["Nejasan broj gostiju"]
  };
  recommended_action: string;  // "Pozovi u roku od 1h"
}

// Example
{
  score: 78,
  conversion_probability: 0.73,
  signals: {
    positive: ["BudÅ¾et: â‚¬500/os", "Datum: 15-22. jul", "Izvor: Facebook Ad"],
    negative: ["Destinacija: 'Svejedno'"]
  },
  recommended_action: "Visok prioritet - pozovi u roku od 30 min"
}
```

### Display in Pipeline

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚ â‚¬500 budÅ¾et                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                         â”‚
â”‚ ğŸ’¡ Visok prioritet - pozovi u roku od 30 min          â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

# 14. TECHNICAL ARCHITECTURE

## 14.1 Database Schema (New Tables)

```sql
-- Offers table
CREATE TABLE offers (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id) NOT NULL,
  
  -- Inventory type (NEW in v2.0)
  inventory_type VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'inquiry', -- 'owned' or 'inquiry'
  
  -- Basic info
  name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  star_rating INTEGER CHECK (star_rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  
  -- Destination
  country VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  city VARCHAR(100),
  
  -- Dates
  departure_date DATE NOT NULL,
  return_date DATE NOT NULL,
  
  -- Pricing
  price_per_person DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  original_price DECIMAL(10,2),
  
  -- Capacity
  total_spots INTEGER NOT NULL,
  available_spots INTEGER NOT NULL,
  
  -- Details
  accommodation_type VARCHAR(50), -- hotel, apartment, villa
  board_type VARCHAR(50), -- all_inclusive, half_board, breakfast, room_only
  transport_type VARCHAR(50), -- flight, bus, none
  
  -- Urgency labels (manual overrides)
  is_recommended BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  
  -- Analytics (for automatic label assignment)
  views_total INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  views_last_24h INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  inquiries_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  booking_rate DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0, -- percentage
  
  -- Status
  status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'active', -- active, sold_out, archived
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Track offer views for "Popularno" label
CREATE TABLE offer_views (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  session_id VARCHAR(255),
  viewed_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Index for fast 24h view counting
CREATE INDEX idx_offer_views_recent ON offer_views (offer_id, viewed_at)
WHERE viewed_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '24 hours';

-- Function to update views_last_24h (run via cron every hour)
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_offer_views_24h()
RETURNS void AS $$
BEGIN
  UPDATE offers o
  SET views_last_24h = (
    SELECT COUNT(*) 
    FROM offer_views v 
    WHERE v.offer_id = o.id 
    AND v.viewed_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '24 hours'
  );
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Offer images
CREATE TABLE offer_images (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  url VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
  sort_order INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Reservations table
CREATE TABLE reservations (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id) NOT NULL,
  offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id),
  lead_id UUID REFERENCES leads(id),
  
  -- Reservation code
  code VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL, -- TRK-2026-001234
  
  -- Customer info
  customer_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  customer_phone VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  customer_email VARCHAR(255),
  
  -- Booking details
  adults INTEGER NOT NULL,
  children INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  child_ages INTEGER[], -- array of ages
  
  -- Pricing
  total_price DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  deposit_amount DECIMAL(10,2),
  amount_paid DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
  
  -- Status
  status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending', -- pending, paid, expired, cancelled, completed
  payment_method VARCHAR(50), -- card_deposit, card_full, agency, contact
  
  -- Timing
  expires_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL, -- 72h from creation
  
  -- Reminders sent
  reminder_24h_sent BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  reminder_48h_sent BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  paid_at TIMESTAMP,
  expired_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Payments table
CREATE TABLE payments (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES reservations(id),
  
  -- Payment details
  amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT 'EUR',
  payment_method VARCHAR(50), -- card, bank_transfer, cash
  payment_provider VARCHAR(50), -- wspay, stripe
  
  -- Provider reference
  provider_transaction_id VARCHAR(255),
  
  -- Status
  status VARCHAR(50), -- pending, completed, failed, refunded
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  completed_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Qualification sessions (for analytics)
CREATE TABLE qualification_sessions (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id),
  
  -- Session data
  session_id VARCHAR(255),
  source VARCHAR(100), -- facebook, instagram, direct, widget
  
  -- Qualification data (JSONB for flexibility)
  qualification_data JSONB,
  
  -- Outcome
  offers_shown INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  reservation_made BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES reservations(id),
  
  -- Timestamps
  started_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  completed_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Offer Inquiries table (NEW in v2.0)
-- For on-request offers where agency must verify with supplier
CREATE TABLE offer_inquiries (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id) NOT NULL,
  offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id),
  lead_id UUID REFERENCES leads(id),
  qualification_session_id UUID REFERENCES qualification_sessions(id),
  
  -- Customer info
  customer_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  customer_phone VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  customer_email VARCHAR(255),
  customer_message TEXT,
  
  -- Status: 'pending' â†’ 'checking' â†’ 'available'/'unavailable'/'alternative'
  status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending',
  
  -- Agent handling
  assigned_to UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  responded_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  responded_at TIMESTAMP,
  response_notes TEXT,
  
  -- If converted to reservation
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES reservations(id),
  converted_at TIMESTAMP,
  
  -- Alternative offered (if original unavailable)
  alternative_offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id),
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Agency settings for booking system
CREATE TABLE agency_booking_settings (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id) UNIQUE,
  
  -- Public page
  slug VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE, -- URL slug: trak.rs/a/[slug]
  logo_url VARCHAR(500),
  primary_color VARCHAR(7), -- hex color
  
  -- Contact
  phone VARCHAR(50),
  email VARCHAR(255),
  address TEXT,
  
  -- Working hours (NEW in v2.0)
  working_hours JSONB DEFAULT '{
    "timezone": "Europe/Belgrade",
    "response_time_working": 10,
    "schedule": {
      "monday": {"enabled": true, "start": "09:00", "end": "18:00"},
      "tuesday": {"enabled": true, "start": "09:00", "end": "18:00"},
      "wednesday": {"enabled": true, "start": "09:00", "end": "18:00"},
      "thursday": {"enabled": true, "start": "09:00", "end": "18:00"},
      "friday": {"enabled": true, "start": "09:00", "end": "18:00"},
      "saturday": {"enabled": true, "start": "09:00", "end": "14:00"},
      "sunday": {"enabled": false, "start": null, "end": null}
    }
  }',
  
  -- Reservation settings
  reservation_hold_hours INTEGER DEFAULT 72,
  deposit_percentage INTEGER DEFAULT 20,
  
  -- Abandoned cart settings (NEW in v2.0)
  abandoned_cart_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  abandoned_cart_discount_percent INTEGER DEFAULT 5,
  abandoned_cart_discount_hours INTEGER DEFAULT 72,
  abandoned_cart_email_1_hours INTEGER DEFAULT 2,
  abandoned_cart_email_2_hours INTEGER DEFAULT 24,
  abandoned_cart_email_3_hours INTEGER DEFAULT 72,
  
  -- Payment settings
  wspay_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  wspay_shop_id VARCHAR(100),
  stripe_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  stripe_account_id VARCHAR(100),
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Bookings table (links leads to offers, tracks all sales)
CREATE TABLE bookings (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id),
  lead_id UUID REFERENCES leads(id),
  offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id), -- NULL if external booking
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES reservations(id), -- if came through Trak flow
  closed_by UUID REFERENCES users(id), -- agent who closed the sale
  
  -- Guest info
  adults INTEGER NOT NULL,
  children INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  child_ages INTEGER[],
  
  -- Financial
  total_amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
  amount_paid DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
  payment_method VARCHAR(50), -- card, cash, bank, mixed
  payment_status VARCHAR(50), -- paid, partial, unpaid
  
  -- External booking info (if offer not in system)
  external_destination VARCHAR(255),
  external_accommodation VARCHAR(255),
  external_dates VARCHAR(100),
  
  -- Status
  status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'confirmed', -- confirmed, cancelled, completed
  
  -- Timestamps
  booked_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  travel_date DATE,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Trigger: Auto-decrement offer capacity on booking
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_offer_capacity_on_booking()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
  IF NEW.offer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
    UPDATE offers 
    SET available_spots = available_spots - (NEW.adults + NEW.children)
    WHERE id = NEW.offer_id;
  END IF;
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE TRIGGER booking_capacity_decrease
AFTER INSERT ON bookings
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE FUNCTION update_offer_capacity_on_booking();

-- Cancellations table (tracks why bookings/leads were lost)
CREATE TABLE cancellations (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id),
  booking_id UUID REFERENCES bookings(id),
  lead_id UUID REFERENCES leads(id),
  
  -- Type
  type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- booking_cancelled, lead_lost
  
  -- Reason
  reason VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  -- booking_cancelled reasons: customer_request, health, changed_destination, financial, agency_cancelled, other
  -- lead_lost reasons: competitor, too_expensive, changed_plans, no_response, dates_unavailable, other
  reason_details TEXT,
  
  -- Refund (for booking cancellations)
  refund_type VARCHAR(50), -- full, partial, none, transferred
  refund_amount DECIMAL(10,2),
  
  -- Timestamps
  cancelled_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  cancelled_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Trigger: Auto-increment offer capacity on cancellation
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_offer_capacity_on_cancel()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
DECLARE
  booking_record RECORD;
BEGIN
  IF NEW.booking_id IS NOT NULL THEN
    SELECT * INTO booking_record FROM bookings WHERE id = NEW.booking_id;
    IF booking_record.offer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
      UPDATE offers 
      SET available_spots = available_spots + (booking_record.adults + booking_record.children)
      WHERE id = booking_record.offer_id;
    END IF;
    -- Update booking status
    UPDATE bookings SET status = 'cancelled' WHERE id = NEW.booking_id;
  END IF;
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE TRIGGER cancellation_capacity_restore
AFTER INSERT ON cancellations
FOR EACH ROW
EXECUTE FUNCTION update_offer_capacity_on_cancel();

-- Abandoned carts table (NEW in v2.0)
-- Tracks customers who completed qualification but didn't book
CREATE TABLE abandoned_carts (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id) NOT NULL,
  qualification_session_id UUID REFERENCES qualification_sessions(id),
  
  -- Contact
  email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  
  -- What they searched for
  qualification_data JSONB NOT NULL,
  
  -- What they saw/clicked
  offers_shown UUID[],
  offers_clicked UUID[],
  
  -- Discount
  discount_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  discount_percent INTEGER NOT NULL,
  discount_expires_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
  discount_used BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  
  -- Email sequence status
  email_1_sent_at TIMESTAMP,
  email_2_sent_at TIMESTAMP,
  email_3_sent_at TIMESTAMP,
  
  -- Outcome
  converted BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  converted_at TIMESTAMP,
  reservation_id UUID REFERENCES reservations(id),
  
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Index for finding carts that need emails
CREATE INDEX idx_abandoned_carts_pending 
ON abandoned_carts (organization_id, created_at)
WHERE converted = false;

-- Lead source tracking (add to existing leads table)
-- ALTER TABLE leads ADD COLUMN source_channel VARCHAR(50);
-- Values: trak_form, facebook_ad, facebook_dm, instagram_dm, 
--         messenger, email, viber, whatsapp, phone, walk_in, other
-- ALTER TABLE leads ADD COLUMN source_raw_text TEXT;
-- Store original message/paste for reference
-- ALTER TABLE leads ADD COLUMN phone_normalized VARCHAR(20);
-- Normalized phone for duplicate detection: +381641234567

-- Notifications table
CREATE TABLE notifications (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id),
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id), -- recipient
  
  -- Content
  type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- new_lead, new_reservation, payment_received, 
                             -- reservation_expiring, reservation_expired, 
                             -- booking_cancelled, new_message
  title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  body TEXT,
  
  -- Reference
  reference_type VARCHAR(50), -- lead, reservation, booking, message
  reference_id UUID,
  
  -- Status
  read BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  read_at TIMESTAMP,
  
  -- Delivery
  email_sent BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  push_sent BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  
  -- Timestamps
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Index for fast unread notification queries
CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_unread ON notifications (user_id, read, created_at DESC)
WHERE read = false;

-- Daily reconciliation log
CREATE TABLE daily_reconciliations (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id),
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  
  reconciliation_date DATE NOT NULL,
  
  -- Stats at time of reconciliation
  leads_created INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  bookings_closed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  revenue_total DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
  
  -- Confirmation
  confirmed_complete BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  confirmed_at TIMESTAMP,
  
  -- If they added bookings after confirmation (tracks honesty)
  bookings_added_after INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  
  -- Notes
  notes TEXT,
  
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  
  UNIQUE(organization_id, user_id, reconciliation_date)
);

-- Weekly capacity audits (manager verification)
CREATE TABLE capacity_audits (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  organization_id UUID REFERENCES organizations(id),
  audited_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  offer_id UUID REFERENCES offers(id),
  
  audit_week DATE NOT NULL, -- Start of week
  
  -- Snapshot at audit time
  capacity_in_system INTEGER,
  bookings_this_week INTEGER,
  bookings_via_trak INTEGER,
  bookings_manual INTEGER,
  
  -- Verification
  verified_correct BOOLEAN,
  corrected_to INTEGER, -- If capacity was wrong, what it was corrected to
  
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);
```

## 14.2 API Endpoints

```
# Public (no auth)
GET    /api/public/agencies/[slug]           # Agency landing page data
GET    /api/public/agencies/[slug]/offers    # List offers for qualification
POST   /api/public/qualify                   # Submit qualification, get matches
POST   /api/public/reservations              # Create reservation
GET    /api/public/offers/[id]               # Single offer details

# Webhooks
POST   /api/webhooks/wspay                   # Payment callback
POST   /api/webhooks/stripe                  # Payment callback
POST   /api/webhooks/facebook                # FB Lead Ads webhook
POST   /api/webhooks/email                   # Inbound email parsing

# Protected (requires auth)
# Leads
GET    /api/leads                            # List leads
POST   /api/leads                            # Create lead (manual)
POST   /api/leads/quick                      # Quick entry (AI parse)
GET    /api/leads/[id]                       # Get lead
PUT    /api/leads/[id]                       # Update lead
POST   /api/leads/[id]/close                 # Close lead (won/lost)

# Offers
GET    /api/offers                           # List agency offers
POST   /api/offers                           # Create offer
GET    /api/offers/[id]                      # Get offer
PUT    /api/offers/[id]                      # Update offer
DELETE /api/offers/[id]                      # Archive offer
POST   /api/offers/import                    # CSV import
PATCH  /api/offers/[id]/capacity             # Quick capacity update

# Bookings
GET    /api/bookings                         # List all bookings
POST   /api/bookings                         # Create booking (direct sale)
GET    /api/bookings/[id]                    # Get booking details
POST   /api/bookings/[id]/cancel             # Cancel booking

# Reservations
GET    /api/reservations                     # List reservations
GET    /api/reservations/[id]                # Get reservation
PATCH  /api/reservations/[id]/status         # Update status
POST   /api/reservations/[id]/extend         # Extend expiry
POST   /api/reservations/[id]/send-reminder  # Manual reminder

# Notifications
GET    /api/notifications                    # List notifications
PATCH  /api/notifications/[id]/read          # Mark as read
POST   /api/notifications/read-all           # Mark all as read

# Inbox (FB/IG messages)
GET    /api/inbox                            # List messages
GET    /api/inbox/[id]                       # Get conversation
POST   /api/inbox/[id]/reply                 # Send reply
POST   /api/inbox/[id]/create-lead           # Create lead from message

# Analytics
GET    /api/analytics/dashboard              # Dashboard stats
GET    /api/analytics/sales                  # Sales report
GET    /api/analytics/sources                # Lead source breakdown
GET    /api/analytics/cancellations          # Cancellation reasons

# Reconciliation
GET    /api/reconciliation/status            # Check if today/yesterday needs reconciliation
POST   /api/reconciliation/confirm           # Confirm day is complete
GET    /api/reconciliation/history           # Past reconciliations
GET    /api/reconciliation/compliance        # Agent compliance stats (manager)

# Capacity Audits (Manager)
GET    /api/audits/pending                   # Offers needing verification
POST   /api/audits/verify                    # Verify or correct capacity
GET    /api/audits/history                   # Past audits

# Settings
GET    /api/settings/booking                 # Get booking settings
PUT    /api/settings/booking                 # Update booking settings

# AI Features (NEW in v2.0)
POST   /api/ai/parse-message                 # Parse Viber/WhatsApp message â†’ Lead data
POST   /api/ai/parse-screenshot              # OCR screenshot â†’ Lead data
POST   /api/ai/score-lead                    # Calculate lead score
GET    /api/ai/match-offers                  # Smart offer ranking for qualification

# Abandoned Carts (NEW in v2.0)
GET    /api/abandoned-carts                  # List abandoned carts
GET    /api/abandoned-carts/[id]             # Get cart details
POST   /api/abandoned-carts/[id]/convert     # Mark as converted
GET    /api/abandoned-carts/stats            # Conversion stats

# Public - Abandoned Cart (NEW in v2.0)
POST   /api/public/email-capture             # Capture email for discount
GET    /api/public/verify-discount/[code]    # Verify discount code is valid
```

| **Agency** | â‚¬199/month | Unlimited everything, White-label, API access, Dedicated support |

# 16. IMPLEMENTATION PHASES

## Phase 1: Core CRM (âœ… DONE)
- Dashboard
- Lead management
- Pipeline
- Basic analytics
- User auth

## Phase 2: Offers Module
- Offers CRUD
- CSV import
- Public catalog page
- Embeddable widget
- Basic inquiry form

**Estimated time: 2-3 weeks**

## Phase 3: Booking System
- Qualification flow UI
- Offer matching
- Reservation system
- Email notifications
- 72h expiration + reminders

**Estimated time: 3-4 weeks**

## Phase 4: Payments
- WSpay integration
- Deposit handling
- Contract PDF generation
- Payment tracking

**Estimated time: 2 weeks**

## Phase 5: Advanced Features
- AI chat qualification
- Facebook/Instagram ad integration
- Advanced analytics
- Multi-language support

**Estimated time: 4+ weeks**

# 17. SUCCESS METRICS

| Metric | Target |
|--------|--------|
| Qualification completion rate | >70% |
| Qualification time | <30 seconds |
| Offer click-through rate | >40% |
| Reservation rate (of clicks) | >25% |
| Payment conversion (of reservations) | >60% |
| Agent response time | <1 hour |

---

# 18. OPEN QUESTIONS

1. **Tour operator partnerships** - Can we get direct data feeds from major operators (Coral, TUI, etc.)?

2. **WhatsApp/Viber integration** - Should reminders go via messaging apps instead of email?

3. **Multi-agency marketplace** - Should there be a public "Trak.rs" where all agency offers are searchable?

4. **Commission model** - Should there be an option for per-booking fee instead of subscription?

5. **Mobile app** - Is a native app needed for agents, or is mobile web sufficient?

# CHANGELOG

## v2.0 - January 13, 2026 â­ MAJOR UPDATE

### Two Inventory Types (Section 2.2)
- `owned` (Sopstveni kapacitet) - Instant booking with 72h hold
- `inquiry` (Na upit) - Agent must verify with supplier
- Results page now shows two sections: "RezerviÅ¡ite odmah" and "Na upit"

### Inquiry System (Section 9.3)
- Inquiry form for on-request offers
- Inquiry confirmation with instant alternatives
- Agent inquiry dashboard
- Status workflow: pending â†’ checking â†’ available/unavailable

### Dynamic Response Time
- Based on agency working hours
- Different messages for: during hours, after hours, weekend

### AI Features (NEW Section 13)
- **Message Parsing** - Viber/WhatsApp text â†’ structured lead data
- **Screenshot OCR** - Image â†’ text extraction â†’ lead parsing
- **Smart Offer Matching** - AI-ranked offers beyond simple filters
- **Lead Scoring** - Conversion probability prediction (0-100)
- **Abandoned Cart Recovery** - Email capture + 3-email sequence with personalization

### Database Schema Updates
- Added `inventory_type` field to offers table
- Added `offer_inquiries` table
- Added `working_hours` JSONB to agency_booking_settings
- Added `abandoned_cart_*` fields to agency_booking_settings
- Added `abandoned_carts` table

### API Endpoints Added
- POST /api/public/inquiries - Submit inquiry
- GET /api/inquiries - List inquiries (agent)
- PATCH /api/inquiries/[id]/status - Update status
- POST /api/inquiries/[id]/convert - Convert to reservation
- POST /api/ai/parse-message - AI message parsing
- POST /api/ai/parse-screenshot - AI screenshot OCR
- POST /api/ai/score-lead - Lead scoring
- GET /api/ai/match-offers - Smart offer matching
- GET /api/abandoned-carts - List abandoned carts
- POST /api/public/email-capture - Capture email for discount

### Other Changes
- Card grid layout for offers (not table/kanban)
- Renumbered sections (Technical Architecture â†’ 14, Business Model â†’ 15, etc.)

## v1.3 - January 9, 2026
- Added Section 10: Trip Management (Aktivni AranÅ¾mani)
  - Trip-centric vs person-centric approach
  - Dynamic trip sections (auto-created on first booking)
  - Person cards with status checklist
  - Trip-level bulk actions
  - Multiple views: by trip, by status, calendar, problems
  - Trip lifecycle management
- Added 14 open questions for Sunday agency meeting
- Renumbered all subsequent sections

## v1.2 - January 9, 2026
- Added Section 9.3: Daily Reconciliation System
  - End of day reminder (17:00 popup)
  - Morning blocker (must confirm yesterday complete)
  - Full day close flow
  - Weekly capacity audit for managers
  - Compliance tracking
- Added database tables: daily_reconciliations, capacity_audits
- Added API endpoints for reconciliation and audits

## v1.1 - January 9, 2026
- Added Section 4: Data Entry & Lead Capture (AI message parsing, quick entry forms)
- Added Section 5: Booking & Closing Flow (quick close, capacity tracking)
- Enhanced urgency labels system with data-driven automatic assignment
- Added 50% label distribution rule to prevent urgency fatigue
- Added cancellation tracking with reasons
- Added notifications system for all events
- Added bookings table with automatic capacity updates
- Added triggers for capacity increment/decrement
- Updated API endpoints for new features
- No overbooking allowed (system blocks)
- Whoever closes gets the sale credited

## v1.0 - January 9, 2026
- Initial specification document
- Complete user flow from ad to payment
- Qualification flow UI
- Offer display with urgency labels
- Reservation system (72h hold)
- Payment integration (WSpay/Stripe)
- Agent dashboard
- Offer management with CSV import
